Phantom was created by Anne Flipo, Dominique Ropion, Loc Dong and Juliette Karagueuzoglou. Top notes are Lavender, Lemon Zest and Amalfi Lemon; middle notes are Lavender, Earthy Notes, Apple, Smoke and Patchouli; base notes are Vanilla, Lavender and Vetiver. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p><strong>PHANTOM, the new fragrance for men by Paco Rabanne</strong></p>

<p>Step into the Paco Galaxy and join an intergalactic party where everyone is invited. Where you can be whoever you want to be. No matter who you are. No matter which planet you come from.</p>


<p>The essence of self-confidence fueled by feel good energies.</p>

<p>A futuristic aromatic fragrance born from the clash between luxury craftmanship and new-tech.Using a cutting-edge creative process to select ingredients to make you feel energized, powerfully confident and sexy.</p>

<p>A bold scent with notes of addictive creamy lavender, fusing energizing lemon and sexy woody vanilla.</p>

<p>Radically different, totally disruptive: PHANTOM is our first connected bottle ever. Tap your phone on its top, and take off with your new wingman!</p>

<p>A bold invitation to step outside the ordinary and celebrate life. 1000% feel-good. 1000% Paco Rabanne.</p>



<p><strong>PHANTOM, beyond perfumery: human emotion, boosted by A.I., crafted in Grasse</strong></p>

<p>How does that work? By matching the luxury craftsmanship of perfumery with new tech. To conceive PHANTOM, Paco Rabanne assembled a dream team of four top-notch perfumers from IFF: Loc Dong for his crazy creativity, Juliette Karagueuzoglou for her exquisite knowledge of natural material, along with the Master Perfumers Dominique Ropion and Anne Flipo for their ability to fine-tune most powerful, long-lasting fragrances ever created by Paco Rabanne.</p>

<p>Their mission: to conceive a feel-good perfume that boosts your sexiness, confidence, and energy. Their super-power: Augmented Creativity, a cutting-edge creative process that uses A.I. to enhance human inspiration and galvanize creativity, applied to perfumery for the first time ever for Paco Rabanne.</p>

<p>Augmented Creativity allowed the quartet to reach beyond their know-how and artistic sensibility. To experiment with unexpected scent pairings. To select the exact ingredients that stimulate sensations of sexiness, confidence, and energy; and fine-tune their dosages. </p>

<p>So, what does it smell like? A match. A clash. A mind-bending, addictive aromatic scent combining an energizing green flash of lemon with ultra-creamy lavender.</p>

<p>The secret ingredient boosting the energy of the lemon accord is a fantastic “vintage” molecule; styrallyl acetate. Scientific measures show that its radiant green fruity facets activate a sense of energy. In PHANTOM, the man-made material is combined with lush natural materials. Zesty lemon peel oil from Italy. Patchouli heart, a slightly smoky earthy note with an apple twist. And a streamlined woody note: vetiver heart.</p>

<p>Jumped up by that energizing green flash, lavender plays it smooth and creamy. Did we say lavender? We meant Lavender 3.0, custom-blended for Paco Rabanne to be irresistibly addictive…  Fresh lavandin heart, crafted for PHANTOM to enhance its most seductive properties. A stellar lavender oil. And organic lavandin absolute enfleurage 2.0 that brings out the ingredient’s most sensuous floral, aromatic, hay-like facets.</p>

<p>Wrap this Lavender 3.0 accord with sexy vanilla absolute and voilà!  Intensely feel-good. Powerfully sexy. Fantastically long-lasting. Now spray and enjoy! You’re all set to party.</p></div><p class="reviewstrigger" style="font-size: smaller; color: #83a6c4">Read about this perfume in other languages: <a padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2304913" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Atomikbomb_"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1211792"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1211792.gif" class="comments-avatar"alt="Atomikbomb_" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2304913ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2304913" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1211792">Atomikbomb_</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-04">10/04/24 13:16</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Like others here, I assumed I would really dislike this fragrance, but I'm happily surprised that I don't! <br />
<br />
I'm not a guy, and although I like a wide range of fragrances, I don't wear truly classically masculine fragrances personally (maybe very rarely, and I believe in wearing what you like regardless of gender marketing, but these are just my preferences). Because of the notes, I thought if I *did* happen to like it, that I could possibly wear it (think Mon Guerlain with vanilla+lavender). But, this retains a decidedly masculine fougere tone from beginning to end. I truly don't understand why this is called "metrosexual" or anything along those lines. As a woman in my 30s, having smelled my share of frags, I think this is easily masculine smelling, and I would find it appealing on men.<br />
<br />
Anyway, it smells crisp when it opens. Really, exceptionally crisp! The citrus is very energizing, and the lavender changes over time within this composition, but initially it smells much more herbaceous than it does as it dries down and softens. <br />
<br />
After a while, the lavender mellows out and becomes smoother. There are tons of variations of natural lavender (I won't geek out about it too much), and while the opening smells of lavandin (which is different/rougher in texture), the drydown smells of French lavender (sweeter). Though, that could be owing to the vanilla. I don't think this vanilla overtakes everything though. Yes, it's sweet, but this never feels gourmond, and it isn't overkill. It's balanced. <br />
<br />
Longevity is pretty decent, and overall, this is far from the worst fragrance Paco Rabanne has put out. I feel that the hate is unwarranted, and felt similarly about "Fame" for women too. Maybe PR is upping their standards? If we disregard the packaging and reputation, smelling this blindly on someone would probably result in much more positive responses.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1246357">ginandrice</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-25">06/25/24 19:25</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Phantom opens with an intensely sweet wallop of candied lemon, licoricey lavender, and warm, creamy vanilla. It's potent and engaging, albeit also rather overwhelming and unsubtle. <br />
<br />
At this stage, the sugared zest of the lemon, and the warm, licoricey spice of the lavender give enjoyable and much-needed dimension to Phantom's core of cake-frosting-esque vanilla. But sadly, it's short-lived, at least on me.  <br />
<br />
On my skin, Phantom dries down papery and chalk-dry within twenty minutes. It still centers on vanillic sweetness at its core, but it becomes much mellower and flatter than it was in the opening. <br />
<br />
Something in Phantom's drydown reminds me of both clay and milled wheat — a dry, warm, monotone powderiness, overlayed by papery sweetness. <br />
<br />
Honestly, my nose very rarely gets along with lavender, so it's really no surprise that Phantom is a miss for me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="68226"comment_id="2199551"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rabanne/Phantom-68226.html?ccid=2199551#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2198080" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2152632">arnii.v</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-02">06/02/24 04:44</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Bought this a few months ago, didn't really like it initially.<br />
This fragrance will get you compliments. It smells like fresh tangerines with a sort of sourness. Lavender note is not very prominent but I would say it's at least somewhat floral. Vanilla slowly fades in and it smells incredible once it does. The fragrance smells best about 45 minutes after spraying, then just slowly gets weaker.<br />
I wore it to class one day and could smell it on myself the entire time. Others around me also noticed. However, I couldn't smell it at the end of the day. The strength and projection is amazing, but the longevity not so much. Very easy to over-spray and this stuff can seriously fill a room for a rather short period of time if one does over-spray. <br />
Definitely not a safe blind buy but also definitely worth testing. Would recommend 8/10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="68226"comment_id="2175391"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rabanne/Phantom-68226.html?ccid=2175391#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2172874" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2151173">Sum Dood</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-30">05/30/24 17:35</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This was actually the first fragrance I ever bought. It was something that I liked at first but now I'm on the fence.<br />
I cant really decide if I like this fragrance or not; sometimes it burns my nostrils, and other times I really like how it smells in the air. It may be too loud for some, and it may get cloyingly sweet at times. But i think that's what makes this fragrance unique. It's 50/50 between being loved or hated.<br />
<br />
The opening is a burst of pineapple and lemon, but quickly dries down to lavender and vanilla. Everything smells synthetic. Not exactly a bad thing, but it can be headache inducing for some. The smell is sweet, young and playful. Longevity depends on how much you spray, but it teeters on moderate and long lasting. The bottle is a big talking point for people since it's a big bulky robot despite the fragrance being called "Phantom".<br />
<br />
Personally, I think I have to be in a certain mood to wear this. It's not something I would wear to a formal event, but it could pass on a casual outing with friends or a simple lunch date. Definitely sample it before you buy it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="68226"comment_id="2172874"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rabanne/Phantom-68226.html?ccid=2172874#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2166674" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;  It's hard for me to rate this perfume.  This composition has a bit of sophistication and niche flair, but I don't like its very cheap, artificial sound.  Unfortunately, the ingredients here are of low quality and this could not be masked.<br />

<br />
It's bright, that lavender and citrus really come through which is supported by the vanilla in the background. I think it's a good fragrance for men 30 and under, of which I am one. <br />
<br />
I think this fragrance works for day and night in warmer weather months, stretching into early Fall. Be careful in hot weather as this can get cloying. Best in spring. <br />
<br />
I have it and bought it before I got really into colognes. Am I glad I have it? Yes. Would I buy another bottle when I run out, probably not.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="68226"comment_id="2138291"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rabanne/Phantom-68226.html?ccid=2138291#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2135741" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; fragrance YouTubers as gospel, i looked at the notes &amp; they're exactly what I wanted but the bad reviews put me off. Finally bit the bullet &amp; got a 50ml &amp; my only regret is not getting the 100ml, sometimes a certain thing can be exactly what YOU want but not others &amp; that's fine it'd be boring if we was all the same! But the way people have talked about this you'd think no one would like it which is just not true. The main thing seems to be "this is for teenagers" but it's a weird assumption considering Lavender is the main note &amp; as a fairly young lad myself I know of 0 teens that would like this because of that, it's more geared to 20-30 year olds in my opinion as it's not overly complex but it's a lot more complex than most 'teen' fragrances, starts sharp &amp; lemony, moves to vanilla &amp; lavender with a tiny bit of apple, then it's a woody lavender drydown but the lemon is always in the background! Someone else said "if this was in a different bottle it'd be a classic" I don't necessarily agree because some people will just not like it, but I do agree that if it had a different bottle &amp; name it'd be taken more seriously but if you're someone that judges fragrances on name &amp; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1689704">trahanj26</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-28">03/28/24 11:48</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I've seen this scent be hated on so much online, whether it be on tiktok, forums, reddit, or here. I for one, never understood the hate.<br />
<br />
The day I first smelled it, I knew what it could deliver. I am yet to meet a woman that does not love when I wear this. I have some of the traditionnal "compliment getters" in my collection and let me tell you that nothing comes close to the amount of compliments this gets. <br />
<br />
It is both intoxicatingly warm and refreshing. The citrus in the openning is delicate, the lavender becomes more and more prominent as the scent dries down. Guys, let me let you in on something, MOST women absolutely LOVE lavender. Pair that with the fresh woodsy scent of the vetiver in the base, you'll get tired of telling women the name that you'll just say "the little grey robot".</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="68226"comment_id="2107076"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rabanne/Phantom-68226.html?ccid=2107076#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2106119" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2106119" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Aromanciamx"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1861446"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Aromanciamx" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2106119ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2106119" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.77); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1861446">Aromanciamx</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-27">03/27/24 13:53</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Quiero empezar esta reseña diciendo que no me gusta hablar mal de los perfumes porque considero que todos están hechos con mucho trabajo y para las persona adecuada cualquier aroma puede ser "El mejor", pero sinceramente yo no disfruto para nada lo que han hecho paco rabanne, jean paul gaultier y carolina herrera en sus últimos lanzamientos, todo me huele igual y con 0 personalidad.<br />
<br />
Considero que no puedes odiar phantom por su aroma, ya que está hecho para gustar a TODO el mundo, mismo motivo por el cual a mi no me gusta. Su aroma es a mi parecer muy similar a invictus y one million (Líneas que no me gustan y nunca voy a entender porque a la gente le gusta tanto) y es que esto es todo menos un perfume revolucionaría. Me gustaría poder vivir y precenciar el momento en que porfin paco rabanne pueda sacar un solo perfume que sea original y para nada similar a sus perfumes o algun otro de la competencia.<br />
<br />
Si te gusta invictus, la linea 212, la linea le male, la linea one million o incluso la línea de Y de YSL este perfume te va a encantar, pero permiteme decirte que hay muchas opciones allá fuera que son mucho más originales y que te podrán volar la tapa del cerebro si les das una oportunidad.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="68226"comment_id="2106119"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rabanne/Phantom-68226.html?ccid=2106119#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2106076" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2106076" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="deadnose"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1792487"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1792487.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="deadnose" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2106076ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2106076" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1792487">deadnose</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-27">03/27/24 13:20</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>@1889616 "manly" fragrances? like Polo Black and The Most Wanted? lol get lost, kid<br />
<br />
One can appreciate what Rabanne was trying to do here and why the robot was apt as a bottle design, given that they used analytics and research studies to come up with data-driven suggestions for ingredients and dosage.  Just like his Paco Rabanne's famous metal dress the maison have *always* engaged in these futuristic avant-garde ventures, daring to do proof-in-concepts even if they don't eventually pan out.<br />
<br />
People ridiculing "AI-made fragrances" should be aware that all the major fragrance companies that source the aromachemicals (and their composers) *already* do this behind the scenes (you likely own one) but Rabanne as far as I know is the first maison that actually admits to the public "this is our goal/this is what we set out to do."<br />
<br />
Nor is there dispute that this is a very sweet composition given that it's lavender on a vanilla base, and that it's targeted to a younger person (18-35) who tends to like compositions in that genre. I'm not into this level of sweet (I'm also over 35 so it wasn't meant for me) but just because it's not for me doesn't mean that this is totally devoid of artistic value.  The negative reviews on this composition are indisputably excessive and unfair given that anyone could easily argue the same about Le Male, Eros, 212/Bad Boy and Toy Boy (especially Toy Boy given the equally cute bottle design)—and yet they get a pass.<br />
<br />
I defend this the same way I would defend one of the thousands (/s) of Montale's "Aouds" (also lol) and Secretions Magnifiques, they clearly have their flaws but indeed that's part of what makes them unique.<br />
<br />
The flaw on this one is the somewhat harsh opening but where it truly counts—the drydown and it's resultant aura—is IMO very pleasant.  Not obnoxious, gently sweet and very long lasting.  Even star composers will create a flop every now and again...but four stars (three of whom are master perfumers) simultaneously signing off on what reviewers think is a failure?  The truth is Loc and Juliette did a great job.  It's meant to be fun and playful, and they nailed it.<br />
<br />
The sharp sweetness in the beginning constantly reminds me of the sticky abrasiveness of L'Envol (Cartier) and the drydown is the sweet non-aromatic half of La Nuit De L'Homme (less the coumarin).  Best of all is the Eros-level strength, you only need one spray so assuming you have a fragrance rotation it'll last you decades.<br />
<br />
Bottle design: apropos to the brief and it really stands out in a collection.  If you have the large one as I do, it's refillable and will definitely be a collectible someday.  You can even strip it of Phantom spirit and fill it with something else if you really wanted to.  It fits in the hand (which is more than I can say for those stupid Guerlain squares that are not meant for a human hand) and delivers a broad mist...which is such a low bar but you'd be surprised how many fragrances fall short of this (Hermès mists).<br />
<br />
One last point - Phantom is not at all a dramatic departure from Rabanne's other offerings like 1 Million and the non-fresh versions of Invictus.  All go to sweet-ville, and each one uses the next road parallel to get there.  What would be shocking is an offering that *didn't* target 18-35.  After all take it from me—you can't be young forever 🙃</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="68226"comment_id="2106076"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rabanne/Phantom-68226.html?ccid=2106076#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2101561" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1892184">Zenith Corvus</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-08">03/08/24 14:19</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>THIS is one of the most hated fragrances? Seriously?!<br />
<br />
Phantom has a pleasant and remarkable blend of lavender, vanilla, and citrus notes. It’s deep, stylish, and can be appreciated by people of various ages; ranging from teenage boys to men in their 40s. It may not be beast mode, but the performance is acceptable. 8–9 hours longevity with a subtle sillage.<br />
<br />
I understand if you dislike Phantom because of the lavender and earthy notes — some people may find them a bit overwhelming when combined — but hating the fragrance solely because of the bottle is absolutely ridiculous. <br />
<br />
I've seen much worse packaging designs among perfumes (not to mention the hideous packaging of Melanie Martinez' Portals perfumes). Having a little robot stand out in my collection is not the end of the world. It’s creative, it’s cute, it’s unconventional, it’s silly, maybe a little childish, but I adore it!<br />
<br />
Phantom may not be every connoisseur’s cup of tea, but at least try to look past the bottle and let the fragrance speak for itself.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2076734" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="TBonetheFella"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1710835"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1710835.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="TBonetheFella" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Jorum-Studio/Spiritcask-79477.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.79477.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Spiritcask"title="Spiritcask"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2076734ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2076734" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.76); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1710835">TBonetheFella</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-28">02/28/24 07:44</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I'll be probably one of the first people to admit on this page: I judged this unfairly based off of others people opinion on this website, and the undeniably tacky bottle it come in. HOWEVER, this has been one of the only scents in my collection that I have repeatedly come back to time and time again.<br />
<br />
This is a super fun, super easy to wear, and playful scent. It falls into a similar vein of fragrance that JPGs "Ultra Male" does, so if you enjoy that you will probably enjoy this. It opens with a very clean and refreshing blast of tart yet slightly candied lemon, like the flesh is candied but the rind is still there, and a super ultra mega creamy lavender. As it dries, it gains a nice crisp granny smith apple note that contrasts against the super creamy and sweet lavender/vanilla combo. This is the part that will probably turn most people off, especially those not fans of super sweet scents, or those who dump 20 sprays on at once. It can be cloying, especially if over sprayed, but if you give it a chance to sit in the air and not immediately go hunting with your nose like a hunting dog, you will probably really enjoy this. From this point on, it's just a linear dry down of the apple/lavender/vanilla drying down more and more until it doesn't scream anymore. <br />
<br />
Overall, I think this is a good alternative scent to JPGs "Ultra Male", as it has the same wonderful sweetness, but with apple and lemon instead of pear. This reads a bit more unisex to me than JPG does, but it's all about what you, yourself like. This is a younger persons scent, or a scent you wear while going out because of how fun and sweet it is.  I know the fragcom mostly hates this scent, and while I own a fair amount of niche fragrances, there is nothing wrong with something that just smells basic and good. <br />
<br />
I bought my 50 mL bottle within the first 2-3 months of it dropping so I really have stellar projection and performance, 2-3 sprays is more than enough or else I choke out everyone in the room, I cannot speak to new formulations. <br />
<br />
6.5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="68226"comment_id="2076734"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rabanne/Phantom-68226.html?ccid=2076734#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2074839" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Dry down smoky then earthy"<br />
<br />
8/10 Me - Wonderful tropical strong fragrance that I could see being amazing in the summer because its very fruity and can smell mango, coconut and tropics. Can't smell lavender/wood much which is surprising as that seems to be what others smell. Really love this, although its only great after dry down. At first, its far too strong, alcoholic and smells a bit like rotten fruit. Earthy after 30 mins</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="68226"comment_id="2008831"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rabanne/Phantom-68226.html?ccid=2008831#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2008372" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1884431">AlbanianTractor</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-12-03">12/03/23 14:11</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Let me start this of by saying that the things that make me love this scent, are mostly the same reasons people despise it: its increadibly sweet, and the vanilla is synthetic smelling. But to me that vanilla blast is very pleasant, and when dried down, it blends well with the other notes. All in all its a really well blended perfume (after the dry down). The lemon smells very fresh and zesty, and accentuates the vanilla really well. The fruity notes (I only realised the apple note, after I saw it here) intertwine with the lavender in a way thats unique to this perfume. The earthy notes, and the smoke give this perfume its masculine edge, but I would classify it  as unisex/more masculine, because these notes are quite faint. <br />
<br />
To me, this scent is best appreciated during spring, and autumn, and is also good during the summer, but I don't wear this during winter. You can get away with, it but it lacks that warm spicyness, that I NEED during those cold days. <br />
<br />
It projects well, and I don't really understand people who find it too loud. I mean if you do 8 sprays, than yeah, it will be noticable, but this isn't even the least bit harsh. It's very sweet, but it leaves room for air, unlike some really cheap women's fragrances. I find this fragrance to be very youthful, definitely check this out if your a teenager who likes sweet scents. I would find it very wierd if my father came home smelling like that.<br />
<br />
The word "compliment getter" gets thrown around a lot by perfume reviewers, but as Phantom is an easy to wear, mass appealing scent, I have gotten several compliments from it. Both my GF and my mother (two separate people) who both hate basically all fragrances love Phantom. Obviously this isn't an increadibly unique, or sophisticated fragrance, but it has its layers, and is really addictive. I can safely say that phantom is in my top 5 designer fragrences. Overall, I'd say that if you enjoy other recent sweet designer fragrances like JPG Scandal for example, you sould definatly give this a try, but this is NOT a safe blind buy.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1983834" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="nihilistgodzillas"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1888837"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1888837.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="nihilistgodzillas" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Ralph-Lauren/Polo-Blue-1198.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.1198.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Polo Blue"title="Polo Blue"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1983834ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1983834" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.78); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1888837">nihilistgodzillas</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-11-23">11/23/23 22:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>You might not like the scent itself but no one can deny how high quality its components are. This is a formula with a note breakdown that I can individually isolate ingredient by ingredient in a vivid manner, and I'm no big nose trained perfume expert. <br />
<br />
Honestly liked it more when I initially got it, gets pretty boring after some usage due to its linearity (although that might be on me). <br />
<br />
I find it very versatile but mostly for daytime wear, although I don't think it goes wrong on any occasion or season.<br />
<br />
I sometimes think of it as the smell of a very expensive car air freshener, in a good way, it's very creamy but energetic, similar to CH Bad Boy Le Parfum but sweeter and with a piercing lavender note instead of that one's equally sharp but kind of unique funky weed note.<br />
<br />
Don't get the hate, only negative is that the performance is nothing to write home about.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="68226"comment_id="1983834"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rabanne/Phantom-68226.html?ccid=1983834#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1978677" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Coming back after half a year and my nose going through a lot of maturing I must say this is still great. I’ve sold it but just recently bought a new one because it was unbelievably cheap and well, I missed it. If I could describe it in one word it would be FUN. <br />
<br />
I’ve tested the parfum flanker and I prefer the fresher og. Phantom isn’t the sexy mysterious guy at the club the parfum was trying to be. He’s the funny guy with uber positive energy and sweet dance moves. Everyone loves him, except the few people standing in the back too prideful to get on the dance floor. <br />
<br />
Now I’ll admit the opening is the best part of this fragrance. The sweet earthy vetiver dry down is still enjoyable, but my god, that citrusy pop in the opening is to die for. Pure party in your nose. And it does indeed have a futuristic vibe. The advertising for this fragrance was spot on. <br />
<br />
Another thing I love about this fragrance is the fact that it perfectly encapsulates the essence of the late great Paco Rabanne. The robot is a nod to pacos metallic and futuristic fashion designs. The juice itself is absolutely wacky but works so well, Pacos vibe exactly. I’m sure he would love this creation. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1331188">RGH01</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-10-20">10/20/23 14:20</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Phantom is a straight up abomination to the world of perfume, a disgustingly synthetic mess. You’ve got this overdose of sneeze-inducing lavender combined with a very earthy apple and vanilla. There’s a head-pounding lemon in there too just to make you more nauseous.<br />
<br />
I don’t even know why I’m taking the time to review this fragrance but words cannot describe how much I dislike it. This fragrance is probably the laziest, dullest and simply the worst excuse for a scent I’ve ever come across.<br />
<br />
As usual with Paco Rabanne the quality of ingredients is abysmal and the blending is atrocious. This truly is a disgusting fragrance made for 13 year old boys who are enamoured by a tacky robot bottle.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="68226"comment_id="1956971"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rabanne/Phantom-68226.html?ccid=1956971#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1954532" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It's a sweet mass appeal scent, like One Million, Le Male etc, two others that get a lot of disdain. I get coconut from it, so it reminds me of holidays abroad, which is never a bad thing. <br />
<br />
I also like the bottle, I'm an '80s kid, I'm duty bound to like toy robots. I can imagine this thing walking about on the floor, falling over He-Man figures.<br />
<br />
Fun fragrance, fun bottle. I think "fun" is a word sadly lacking in the vernacular of a lot of folk that take smelly wet stuff a little bit too seriously, not everything has to be a masterpiece niche in an elegant bottle. Paco Rabanne especially seems to get a boatload of hate yet they're very popular - maybe that's the issue, gate keepers not liking things that normal people like? I dunno. I just see a lot of snobbery around and hating on something that's essentially just a vessel for making us smell nice seems a waste of energy. This sits proudly on one of my shelves along with all the other 'ugly' bottles the frag God's sneer at, like the Police skulls, JPG Kokorico, Toy Boy Teddy, Watts light bulbs etc. Heck, if I were a woman I'd even have the Herrera stilettos on there as well.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1928448" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="kittenpawz"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1784272"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1784272.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="kittenpawz" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Ariana-Grande/Ari-31661.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.31661.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Ari"title="Ari"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1928448ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1928448" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1784272">kittenpawz</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-09-15">09/15/23 05:30</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I got a sample of Phantom with another purchase.<br />
My mom has been using Mr. Clean Antibacterial Cleaner With Summer Citrus since forever, triggering my lifelong  intolerance to lemon scented chemical liquids. It's my ultimate "hell no!" scent from childhood. This is that + a hint of lavender + very realistic lemon zest and no they're not the same, lemon is juicy and on the sour side whereas zest is bitter and dry. People who eat a lot of citrus fruits like oranges smell this way, and it has absolutely nothing to do with sexiness and confidence like the brand claims. It's "Bart, can we stop for lemons?" kind of citrus fragrance, something you'd expect from Moschino perhaps - a Fresh Couture scent for men; the bottle is also Moschino worthy, they usually go for quirky designs like this. You could say "I've smelled this somewhere before" and be correct because it smells like a very ordinary, linear, affordable, done-a-thousand-times-before male fragrance with extra citrus, or like a teenage boy's deodorant. Maybe it would be sweet for someone who normally goes for chypres or fougeres but I prefer gourmands and don't find it sweet. <br />
<br />
The idea of an AI-made fragrance is ridiculous to be honest and would only work if people could make their own custom-tailored fragrances that way, for fun or the sake of experiment, kind of like "build your own sandwich" at Subway. Many perfumers have their signature touch that we look for when sampling their new creations, and to be recognized as a perfumer means to have your artistic expression valued by many people. The art of perfumery is declining as is and we need not take another step in that direction. Imagine going 100 years back in time to tell Jean Carles or Jacques Guerlain that in 2020s fragrances will be created by robots, they would be horrified.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; I don't understand all of this hate for an 80's-style toy robot design!...🤷🏾♂️<br />
Firstly, the 80's was THE best era! Fashion was it's best, music was it's best, television was superb.<br />
It was ALL about feeling and good times... and people ALL looked like they loved it, not at-all like today, where we're being forced to go along with blatant agenda's, that are thrust upon you daily, hourly through media.<br />
<br />

I'm absolutely sure that's what it is, because WHO CARES what a fragrance bottle looks like, as long as the fragrance is nice, attractive, well-blended and performs well!? I haven't even seen hatred and outrage for a fragrance. Even this one!... and it's pretty BAD - it smells like a Car Tree air-freshener or shoe polish.<br />

I've honestly NEVER ever thought to myself (about ANY fragrance) "oo, I love this, but I hate the bottle!" NEVER!<br />

This bottle is the coolest-looking one on my shelf.<br />
O.G 1 Million and Lucky look very good, also.<br />
About Armaf CDN bottles... thought, "damn, these are kinda tacky and cheap-looking!..." and admittedly, i didn't want them on my perfectly uniformed, well-organised, well-arranged shelf, because they're extremely poor quality and look as such.<br />
I cannot explain it; it's not the design or anything. They just look as though they're cheaply made.<br />
This however, looks like a toy from Stranger Things, or an 80's Tomy toy robot. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1257945">DobriAndonov</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-09-06">09/06/23 03:35</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>When it came out, I've asked a friend of mine to decant me 10ml of it. Tried it several times. And it is not that intriguing.<br />
<br />
The opening is tenable. Not good, not bad. Kinda strange and chaotic with a decent lack of completion. But still tenable.  <br />
<br />
The strange thing comes after. When it start dries down, it becomes more and more familiar with something. Until the complete drydown when it happens to be 'This is him' by Zadig &amp; Voltaire. The resemblance is drastic for me, but the Phanton is somewhat toothless and blunted.<br />
<br />
The scent is okay. The longevity is moderate, as much as the sillage and the projection. I will rather buy a new bottle of This is Him than a full bottle of this one. The potence of the Z&amp;V is much higher and the smell is more alluring.<br />
<br />
In total: Phantom is good, but nothing more. If I was younger, I could've bought it because of the bottle. But nowdays .. nah! Totally skipping it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="68226"comment_id="1920961"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rabanne/Phantom-68226.html?ccid=1920961#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1920843" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1901974" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="NoirMemoir"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1329296"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1329296.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="NoirMemoir" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Flame-52180.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.52180.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Eros Flame"title="Eros Flame"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1901974ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1901974" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1329296">NoirMemoir</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-08-14">08/14/23 09:28</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>After more then a few...less flattering reviews and impressions, i got a sample and was eager to hate it. I opened the package and, excited, one by one i took out each sample. When i got Phantom in my hand i squinted my eyes, frowned, then put it away thinking "In the corner with you, where you belong!"<br />
<br />
Today i took out this black sheep, middle child of a fragrance out of the corner for a first impression. First spray and a cold, metalic, synthetic blast suckerpunched me, HARD! This thing unclogged my synuses like a syringe full of saline!<br />
<br />
After the sting subsided, this sharp, sugary, lemony scent reminded me of a cocktail made by a child fooling around. He put some lemon peel in it, a bag of skittles, and pretty much all the sugar and sweeteners he could get his little hands on from the kitchen . Politely you take a sip, act like it tastes good, then pour it in the sink when he's not looking.  Im thinking, im gonna have a field day on this one! First fragrance i would actually hate! <br />
<br />
But then it settled, started to dry down and lose the sharp edges. Sweetness took over and calmed things down, with the lemon still present. There's something else in this that makes it odd. That must be the Earthy / Smokey note, but the more it dries down on my hand, the more i like it! <br />
<br />
Its a sweet and youthful fragrance no doubt, but lemony sweet, and that makes it a pretty refreshing scent overall. Its a synthetic scent but thats not an inherently bad thing, and i can easily tell that its a compliment machine (robot?). After the myriad of modern redundant ambery sweet datenight-ish designer fragrances i tested recently, this is a nice change of pace.<br />
<br />
I might even pick up a bottle of this, if i can somehow get past the presentation. Because f... that robot man! padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1790803">parvatishallow</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-07-25">07/25/23 06:51</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This fragrance is a mess, yeah. I kind of like it for what it is though.<br />
<br />
TLDR: Citrus dominated fragrance with a pretty messy smoky/earthy note.<br />
<br />
On opening, it's zesty and very strong. Not unpleasant and it's also not cloying to me whatsoever. It gets messy when the earthy, smoky notes start hitting. Then it begins to smell kind of awful. Like a straw hat that has been soaked in dirt and cheap shampoo. As it dries down, it's fine. You start getting more of the vanilla base and the lemon is still pretty prevalent. I just wish the earthy notes weren't included in this. The sillage on this is probably better than smelling it directly. I've noticed that Fame and Phantom both share a very creamy smelling base. They're more similar than you'd probably expect.<br />
<br />
Not a safe blind buy, masculine, super smoky, and probably better for the spring or fall.<br />
<br />
VISUAL: a lemon on a plate, with vanilla extract, topped with wood shavings and cigarette ash.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="68226"comment_id="1886568"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rabanne/Phantom-68226.html?ccid=1886568#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1885866" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; The vanilla, citrus, and lavender combine to give the melon-like first impression. It all blends together nicely and remains fresh throughout the dry down. <br />
<br />
 If it wasn't for the bottle, this would be a much higher rated fragrance, as this is a very nice, wearable scent. This is definitely a flirty scent in line with Eros, Le Male and Most Wanted although this is the most broadly wearable of all of these IMO. This would work in a casual school/office environment but is a bit too sweet for anything formal.<br />
<br />
8/10 scent for me. I can honestly see myself picking this up for a date night scent as most of what I have is office/oriented. As others have mentioned, this is a very underrated scent that smell great and is slightly more versatile than Eros, Le Male, etc.<br />
<br />
After wearing the sample quite a few more times, I have to bump it up to an 8.5/10. It's just a really nice, pleasant, well-done scent.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="68226"comment_id="1869492"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rabanne/Phantom-68226.html?ccid=1869492#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1869376" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Somehow I never realized how exceptional it is. Exceptional because its earthiness is, on me, very complimentary as I adore both lavender and Vetiver; both spring from the depths of what my soul gives to the universe, and as such, I might wear it to party — anywhere! Anytime! Any place, and any how. I love it and am unapologetically immersed in its captivating appeal. I’ll admit vetiver, patchouli, and lavender is an acquired taste; but, who knew? The key is to wear this fragrance with a sense of dignity. While I couldn’t wear it to the office because it’s too provocative, I would wear it to church Maundy Thursday, Good Friday, or Christmas Eve Night Mass. The such occasions Phantom subtly lives up to its name, but does not steal the show!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="68226"comment_id="1862524"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rabanne/Phantom-68226.html?ccid=1862524#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1860868" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I hadn't tried it yet inside a store or anything so I expected a very sweet and similar scent to other Paco Rabanne frags. At first I thought I was right and just continued on the day with the scent on my arm. Couple hours later to be surprised with something so nice. The scent gets better when it dries down to the more earthy and darker notes while still having that sweetness in the background. The vanilla is really nice, I really enjoy vanilla fragrances so that ticks another box for me. I've never hated the bottle, it's so funny and a little tacky, but who cares. No one is going to see the bottle on you anyway.<br />
<br />
Sweet fragrance, so I think sweet haters won't love this either. I think people hate on it for the bottle more than the fragrance.<br />
<br />
Where to use?: I've heard people use this as their signature, because you can use it in any weather. It has fresh notes, sweet notes and darker/earthy notes. More of a winter/fall fragrance for sure though. BUT I've already used it once this summer and I was surprised that I actually got a couple compliments. To me this is like a party fragrance, go clubbing, out with friends, drinking, that type of stuff.<br />
<br />
I wouldn't buy it for myself though, because I don't (or wouldn't) use it that often. Still, good stuff.<br />
<br />
Edit: I've now realized it isn't for winter, been using this while out with people. The projection is not good, wouldn't recommend really. <br />
While orange isn't listed in the notes, I swear Phantom smells like an orange creamsicle with subtle lavender, smells very edible and tasty.<br />
Where I see the amount of hate this gets, I can't say I'm surprised since it's pretty linear and one-dimensional, but it doesn't stop it from smelling nice.<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1702817">Sweetboy05</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-03-09">03/09/23 00:27</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I don't get the hate for this. The scent is fine, I don't care what anyone says. Y'all wanna get on these sites and complain that companies are putting out boring, generic that lack depth, inspiration, CHARACTER, (that's laughable) and whatever else you want to call it. You want something original, and while this may not be original in terms of smell, at least there's the bottle. I mean, how many fragrances do you see with a bottle design like this? There are plenty of original scents out there. After all, that's what starts a line in the first place and gets itself flankers. *GASPS!* An ORIGINAL SCENT! *THE HEAVENS OPEN UP AND THE ANGELS SING THE PRAISES OF PERFUMERY*. And the scent itself is not as bad as people are making it out to be. You don't have to like it, but to me, it's good. There's only so much perfumers can do with notes in the world of fragrances. There's only so many note combonations they can put together to make these wonderful pieces of art that take a lot of time and effort for you fragheads to just crap on them. They have to think about how they're gonna make the fragrance, gotta think about the ingredients, the oils, the tools, the process, the time, the bottle design, etc. There's so much more to perfumery than what you think. Maybe if you take a moment and stop caring so much about "inspiration", "character," "depth", blah blah blah, (still laughing about that) and take and appreciate it for what it is, you'd probably find there is nothing wrong with and that your nose is just biased or whatever. So either take the fragrance or leave it. Y'all keep raising your expectations higher and higher without regard to how much pressure you can put on these perfumers, (and this can applied to other things with devoted, die-hardcore fanbases, like TV-shows, movies, books, stuff like that.) And is it really all that surprising that brands have lost their "creativity"? At this point in time, it's getting harder and harder for these brands to do anything really NEW. There have already been tons and tons of scent profiles and DNA's that have been explored. There are literally THOUSANDS of fragrances out there. What else can they do? What else can perfumers think of? What other kind of note combonations are truly unique? What else is there? They (kinda) know that they're making them for you, as well as the general public, which, we all know is the MAIN demographic they're going for ANYWAY.  IT'S CHEMICALLY SCENTED WATER IN A BOTTLE! WHAT ARE YOU ALL FUSSING ABOUT!? <br />
Anyway, I'm done with my little rant. <br />
<br />
<br />
<br />
edit: I did not write this post to come at anyone or sound hateful in any way. This is just hatred towards particular fragrances I've observed over time and I finally went ahead and registered myself in to write my own reviews. I am not surprised. It smells like 90% of the sweet designers on the shelf. Don’t even know why I bother to write this review because it is nothing to write about, just the same old story repeating itself. It is the story of Invictus, Ultramale, Stronger with you, Bad Boy, Y etc etc, and if you are into those, you will probably like this. But if you have any of those, you’ll not need this. Generic, cheap and a total lack of creativity. Its a copy of a copy of a copy. And four famous parfumers got their name on this uninspiring blend which is generated by an algoritm. Where is the integrety? Listen to this about why Paco chose the parfumers:<br />
<br />
«Loc Dong for his crazy creativity, Juliette Karagueuzoglou for her exquisite knowledge of natural material…».<br />
<br />
They are on board because of their «Crazy creativity» and «knowledge of natural materials». Let me put it this way. Natural materials and creativity are not what comes to mind when smelling Phantom. My first thought was «this is the generic DNA I have smelled many, many times before».<br />
<br />
The marketing and bottle are just gimmick. Big no from me. Obviously. <br />
<br />
To finish with some positivity. There are many easy to like niche fragrances at the same price point as designers like Phantom. Its a myth that all niche is so expencive compared to designers. Explore and you may discover new worlds and get inspired to have one of the greatest and best smelling hobbies in the universe.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex;
